# Cycle log — append-only

Every problem-attempt cycle gets one row. Failures count. Cherry-picking is forbidden by `.claude/rules/cycle-discipline.md`.

## Schema

| Column | Notes |
|---|---|
| `cycle_id` | sequential integer |
| `problem` | P{id}-{slug} |
| `start_score` | best score we held entering the cycle (or `none` for first attempt) |
| `end_score` | best score after the cycle |
| `hours` | wall-clock spent on the cycle (rough; cap at 100h) |
| `compute` | local-cpu / local-mps / modal / mixed / local-cpu+llm / none-strategy-only / none-placeholder (autonomous_loop scaffold rows) |
| `wiki_citations` | # of wiki/ pages we cited during the cycle |
| `findings_added` | # of new wiki/findings/ pages produced |
| `concepts_added` | # of new wiki/concepts/ pages produced |
| `author_mix` | agent/human/hybrid counts |
| `outcome` | conquered / improved / no-change / new-finding-no-improvement / blocked |
| `notes` | one-line gloss |
| `cites_src` | count of `docs/source/<file>.md` paths the inner agent declared informed this attempt. Full per-cycle path list at `mb/logs/cited-sources.jsonl`; promotion candidates (≥3 cites cross-cycle) at `mb/logs/promotion-candidates.md`. Added 2026-05-25 per Goal 4 of `js/feat/research-synthesis`. Rows before that date predate the column. |

| 1 | P19 difference-bases | 2.6390274695 → 2.6390274695 | ~1.5 | local-cpu | 8 (strategy + literature + 3 questions + 3 concepts) | 1 (`dead-end-p19-different-k-local-search.md`) | 0 | a:1/h:0/hyb:0 | new-finding-no-improvement | `js/research/p19-difference-bases` — Cycle 1, H1' (different-k local search around SOTA k=360). Refined from council H1 after Step 1 read of prior strategy.md. Tested k=358 (best v=16022), k=359 (best v=16210), k=361 strategic single-add (best v=49179). All NEGATIVE: SOTA basin is rigid structural minimum for local moves. Combined with prior w=3 BnB exhaustive lemma, the 7-way SOTA tie is a deep structural floor. Original H1 (different R'), H2 (LP/SDP cap), H3 (algebraic constructions) deferred to follow-up branches per stop-condition (b). |
| 2 | P19 difference-bases | 2.6390274695 → 2.6390274695 | ~1.0 | local-cpu | 5 (concepts + personas + cycle-1 finding) | 2 (`cross-pollination-not-compute.md` meta-principle, `p19-kronecker-bridging-threshold.md` structural insight) | 0 | a:1/h:0/hyb:1 | new-finding-no-improvement | `js/research/p19-difference-bases` — Cycle 2, Spec C (cross-block coverage scaling). Triggered by user's "cross-pollinate not compute" reframing during cycle 1 review. Filed the meta-principle as a hybrid-authored wiki finding (transferable to all 23 problems). Cross-block analysis on SOTA revealed: formula `v = L·λ + c(A)` is a CONDITIONAL identity with bridging threshold `c(A) ≥ λ − max(A) − 1`. SOTA saturates this threshold exactly (c(A)=1043, λ−max(A)=1044). Refines prior framing: lever is joint `(c(A), λ, max(A))`, not c(A) alone. Opens cycle-3 direction: tune max(A)↑ and c(A)↓ jointly in extended-span design space. |
| 3 | P19 difference-bases | 2.6390274695 → 2.6390274695 | ~0.3 | local-cpu | 3 (cycle-2 finding + concepts) | 1 (`dead-end-p19-extended-span-1-swap.md`) | 0 | a:1/h:0/hyb:0 | new-finding-no-improvement | `js/research/p19-difference-bases` — Cycle 3, extended-span 1-swap test (the concrete direction cycle 2 surfaced). Tested 93,870 swaps `(x → y)` with `y ∈ [6968, 8010]` (1010 new y values prior 1-swap never tested). Result: 0 swaps even PRESERVE c(A) at 1043; every swap strictly drops c(A). Combined with prior 1-swap [0, 7000] and w=3 BnB exhaustive: NO 1-swap of A_sota with y ∈ [1, 8010] reaches c(A) ≥ 1044. Refines cycle 2: the rigidity isn't about the bridging-threshold formula; it's about the diff-multiset being globally tight in a way single-mark perturbations cannot navigate. Cycle 4 candidates: 2-swap with extended span, OR pivot to other cross-pollination threads (Saarela-Vanhatalo / OT / B-T inversion). |
| 4 | P19 difference-bases | 2.6390274695 → 2.6390274695 | ~0.2 | local-cpu | 2 (cycle-2 finding + concepts/kronecker) | 1 (`dead-end-p19-4mark-sidon-rulers.md`) | 0 | a:1/h:0/hyb:0 | new-finding-no-improvement | `js/research/p19-difference-bases` — Cycle 4, non-perfect 4-mark Sidon ruler enumeration (council H1 original question). Enumerated 114 4-mark Sidon rulers up to c=12; tested each with `B = A_sota ⊕ λ·R'`. Result: SOTA's `R = {0,1,4,6}` is uniquely best (along with mirror `{0,2,5,6}`). Non-perfect 4-mark rulers with gaps in (R-R)+ collapse v to ≤ 41098 (because missing shells aren't bridged at the SOTA atom's max(A)=6967). Closes "different 4-mark R'" question (at fixed atom A_sota). Cycle 5 candidate: 5-mark non-perfect Sidon rulers (forces |A|=72, larger L=11 potential, but requires max(A) ≥ λ for missing-shell bridging — needs custom atom construction, fresh branch). |

| 12 | P19 difference-bases | 2.6390274695 → 2.6390274695 | ~0.6 | local-cpu | 6 (bridging-threshold finding + 3 prior dead-ends + concepts/kronecker + p19 problem index) | 1 (`dead-end-p19-from-scratch-extended-span.md`) | 0 | a:1/h:0/hyb:0 | new-finding-no-improvement | PR #82 — `js/research/p19-bridging-threshold`. Surfaced two corrections to cycle 2: (a) Wichmann perfect rulers exist at k=4r+3 only, not k=90 — the predicted "c ≈ 1500 in span 7500" is structurally wrong (empirically c ≤ 65 at k=90 for both Pegg/Wikipedia gap formulations); (b) the 2-axis bridging Pareto `(c, max)` is in tension at k=90 — best k=90 sparse rulers have `max ≈ c ≤ 2000` (perfect-ruler regime), but shell-to-shell bridging requires max ≥ 4005, forcing wasted marks that collapse c. SOTA's `(max=6967, c=1043)` sits on this frontier. Promoted `atom_bnb.py` from `mb/.../private-scripts/` to public `cb/scripts/difference_bases/atom_bnb.py` (fixed post-refactor SOTA_PATH).
